I have watched Coach Phil on many occassions and there is only one thing to say about SCNF......THIS PLACE IS AWESOME! Teaching young kids to perform physical feats is one thing but teaching them how to overcome inner obstacles is truly a God given talent.
Specifically, Coach Phil, is able to take time out from the chain of coaching tasks that consumes his time and will undertake a process of learning each youth member in his program, a process that is more often carried out on the run rather than in quiet seclusion. He is able to help the youth dig below the barriers of their fears or hesitations and refocus on the core values and principals that make the individual character strong. Once he has achieved this the youth in his program see and sense those values and principles and gain a renewed sense of purpose which acts as a springboard for confidence, discipline and strength of spirit.
By repeating this process again and again through their workouts or daily lives these youth are able to craft an authentic and strong identity based on who they are and not what someone else's understanding of who they are or should be. In this way, through his coaching and core value influences, they begin to make the transition from being a timid follower to becoming a confident American Ninja Warrior and maybe even tomorrow's leaders.< /text>

We really enjoyed the food,  very tasty.  The service was excellent.  The quality of the food is excellent.  The waitress was very helpful with suggestions of very tasty dishes.  We could also order dishes not on the menu such as "Chinese Broccoli with Hoisin Sauce",  one of our favorites usually not on the menu at most Chinese restaurants.  We also found the prices  reasonable for the quality and quantity of the food.  We will be returning. Also, the one bad review was because the restaurant only had canned soda and didn't offer refills. I don't go to a good Chinese restaurant to drink soda. They give you all the  tea and water you want.< /review>

< text>
Most chinese restaurants I've been to, you would expect your entree in a simple platter. Not this place.  I ordered the Dragon and Phoenix and expected just that but these folks went all out to make an art show with their presentation.  The food is great, prices are appropriate and wait times are minimal. Their "dinner for one" option is perfectly portioned so that you can eat half of the entree and be satisfied while bringing the rest home for a second bite. Bottom line, I like this place and will come by more often.< /text>

< review>
Really enjoyed our stop here.  We tried every beer but 1 on the menu and they were all above average I think.  The standout was their Double IPA for me and we walked away with a few 4 packs.  The seating situation was good too, they had a nicely appointed indoor section, a patio section just outside the taproom, and then another section out on the street.  So plenty of seating.  The beertender was cool and seemed to have a good idea of what beers we may prefer.</review>

< review>
3 mile just turned 2 years old, and over that span the brewery has quickly become a staple of downtown Davis. The beers are good, there's plenty of bike parking on G street, and Three Mile trivia is the best around.

My favorite beer here is the Portland Dark, but when that isn't in tap I tend to go with the Mo-Mosaic, probably their best consistent offering.</review>

<Gmap_id>0x808529748060ba75:0x35da46839d451e2a< /Gmap_id>< review>
This was a great place to visit.  Was in town for work and searched out breweries in Davis.  I love supporting the smaller breweries, especially recent startups.  At the time of my visit (March 2016), I don't think they had even been open for a month, but by 10:00 PM, this place was hopping!  I got two sampler flights (four small glasses of beer in each flight) so I was able to try all eight of their available beers, all eight were great.  No food served here, but you can order in or pick up food and bring it in from the numerous places within walking distance.  I picked up some food from Blaze Pizza (other side of the block) and had that along with the great beer while sitting at the cool concrete bar that one of the owners made.  This place has both inside and outside seating available (when it's not full).  I was in on a Friday night, so that may have contributed to the level of patrons.

Fun place and great beer.  If I'm back in town, I'll be coming back to this brewery!</review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
These guys roast their own beans and keep it real simple. Oat or Almond milk are your only two options but I don't mind as I love the Oatly brand milk with my coffee. Their Cool Beans blend is what I've had both times I've been here. A bright blend that has my beloved Ethiopian bean in it. Coffee is prepared well and I can always taste the notes. Parking is metered but I've gotten a spot both times I've come down here during the week in the middle of the day. The owner is passionate about the craft and for the 3rd wave coffee lover, you won't be disappointed here!<//Review>

Tower Mart has easily the best fried chicken of any similar place. It's much better than KFC and on par with Popeyes for a fraction of the price. So so good, my wife and I get it several times a month, or even more frequently.

The staff are always very friendly and polite. The store and restrooms are always clean. They have a great selection of snacks and drinks.

It's right across the street from 711, which means there's no reason to stop there if Tower Mart is open.</review>

I am speechless. This store and their manager, Leo, are the worst. My husband and I were in the process of moving and needed to get new phones and lines. Leo was the one who set up our new account/plan and we thought we were being taken care of. He was outgoing, friendly, very personable and he even generously waived the activation fees. During our account set up he even informed us that Sprint Complete, which is their phone insurance, was mandatory for all new lines. He then gave us a free Sprint Drive and a Tracker and said that it was no charge because it was Sprints gift to us...

It turns out there was a charge on our next bill for the Tracker and Sprint Drive, unbenounced to us. We were then billed the activation fees that he had said he'd "waived". Our first bill was about $140, less than what was agreed on so we were happy. Our second bill was TRIPLE that!! When my husband got the email for the second bill, he went to visti our local corporate Sprint store in a different area. We were completely confused as to why the bill was so high; we needed some clarity. They proceeded to confirm our bill with him and said that our bill was higher due to the MONTHLY charges of the Sprint Drive and Tracker, the activiation fees for both phones, and the Sprint Complete insurance (which by the way is NOT mandatory)!! Leo LIED to us. He took advantage of me and my husband. He told us that we wouldn't get charged and tried to hide the charges by adding them to a separate bill he thought we wouldn't check. When my husband tried to call the Lompoc store, Leo "wasn't there". A helpful Sprint employee immediately called after alluding to be a customer and Leo was suddenly on the phone and ready to help set up his new account. Leo then proceeded to tell us that my husband and I wanted the products and that we were aware of the added charges, which we were not nor did we agree to them. Good thing Sprint's customer care for FRAUD was nice enough to credit our bill for the outrageous charges that were billed because of Leo greediness.

I wish I could give this store 0 stars but since I have to, it gets 1. I see from other reviews that Leo has done this before and I wish I had checked this before going in. I hope that our situation gets resovled peacefully and so far our local Sprint store and the company have been helpful as well as gracious. To anyone else that Leo may have tried to swindle, or if he's lied to you/taken advantage of you, I hope you'll be courageous enough to stand up to this fraud of a "manager".</review>

< review>
Gotta say this is one busy Micky D's. I was  going to pass this place up upon my initial impressions because how crowded it was in the morning. For real, the parking lot is double most or triple some McDonads and it was almost to full capacity. Then the drive-thru lines had about 10 vehicles in line wrapping around to the street. Well, to my surprise the line inside was super quick! I was in and out in a snap :-)

What I liked...
* Nice new looking remodel.
* Super large parking lot with easy parking.
* Preparation of food was very fast given the amount of customers in the morning rush.
* It was an extra bonus that both the employees and store patrons were unusually friendly and smiling. That's not the reputation Long Beach has, but certainly nice to see :-)

What I didn't like...
* Nothing comes to mind.

Food = as expected
Service = friendly
Seating area = very clean</review>

Still, this joint is busy all day long, especially at the traditional lunch and dinner times. However, this particular iteration of the franchise really tends to be well-kept, maintained and the service is above average for fast-food chains of this calibre(most of all, McDonald's, because so many of the franchise's locations survive strictly on name). I have had very good experiences with the employees here for the most part. And the crusty-looking riff-raff crawling across the town somehow doesn't assert a distracting presence here as they often do at low-cost, high-volume establishments.
